                    (function() {
                        if(window.innerWidth >= 1550){
                            $('#leftStaticSlot').removeClass('hidden');
                            var repositionStaticVertical2 = () => {
                                let elmntWidth = 1220;
                                let windowWidth = window.innerWidth;
                                let horizontal = (windowWidth-elmntWidth)/2-170;
                                $('#leftStaticSlot').css('left', horizontal);
                            }
                            $(window).resize(repositionStaticVertical2);
                            repositionStaticVertical2();
                        
                            if(window['nitroAds']){
                                window['nitroAds'].createAd("leftStaticSlot", {"floor": 0.2, "refreshLimit": 10, "refreshTime": 30, "sizes": [[160,600]], "report":{"enabled":true,"wording":"Report Ad","position":"bottom-right"}});
                            } 
                        } 
                    })();
                </script>

        <div class="infobannerContent">
                            <a href="https://porofessor.gg/download?utm_source=log-website&amp;utm_medium=infobanner" target="_blank" class="content" onclick="WgHelpers.sendGaEvent('InfoBanner', 'OWAppBanner clicked', null); ">
                
                Get this data directly in the client. <button><i class="fa fa-windows"></i> Download the Porofessor app</button>
                                </a>
            
                            <span class="closeButton right" onclick="infobanner.closeInfoBanner('OWAppBanner')">
                    <i class="fa fa-cancel"></i>
                </span>
                    </div>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        var Infobanner=(function(){function Infobanner(bannerId){this.infobannerId=bannerId;if(!this.getIsClosedBannerCookie()){this.showClosableInfoBanner();}}
        Infobanner.prototype.closeInfoBanner=function(){var _this=this;var closed=this.doCloseInfoBanner();if(closed){this.setClosedBannerCookie();setTimeout(function(){return WgHelpers.sendGaEvent('InfoBanner',_this.infobannerId+' closed','');},1000);}};Infobanner.prototype.showClosableInfoBanner=function(){var banner=$('#'+this.infobannerId+'.closable');if(banner.length>0){banner.css('display','block');return true;}else{return false;}};Infobanner.prototype.doCloseInfoBanner=function(){var banner=$('#'+this.infobannerId);if(banner.length>0){banner.css('display','none');return true;}else{return false;}};Infobanner.prototype.setClosedBannerCookie=function(){this.setCookie(this.infobannerId+"_closed","1",365);};Infobanner.prototype.getIsClosedBannerCookie=function(){return!!this.getCookie(this.infobannerId+"_closed");};Infobanner.prototype.getCookie=function(name){var i,x,y,ARRcookies=document.cookie.split(";");for(i=0;i<ARRcookies.length;i++){x=ARRcookies[i].substr(0,ARRcookies[i].indexOf("="));y=ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf("=")+1);x=x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");if(x==name){return unescape(y);}}
        return null;};Infobanner.prototype.setCookie=function(name,value,days){var expires;if(days){var date=new Date();date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));expires="; expires="+date.toUTCString();}else{expires="";}
        document.cookie=name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";};return Infobanner;}());
        var infobanner=new Infobanner('OWAppBanner');
    </script>
